***strijdwagen.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:strijdwagen.html>strijdwagen</a> (37709)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:strijd.html>strijd</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">battle</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:wagen.html>wagen</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">wagon</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. First attested in the seventeenth century.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:strijdwagen.html>strijdwagen</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:strijdwagens.html>strijdwagens</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:strijdwagen.html>strijdwagentje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li>chariot
<ul><li><b>1626</b>, Joost Vondel, <i><a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>De</a> Amsteldamsche Hecvba. Treur-Spel</i>, act III, lines 605-608.
<dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Latn e-quotation" lang="nl">Ghy <a href = vnd.unilang:hebt.html>hebt</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:oud.html>oud</a> Troien <a href = vnd.unilang:thans.html>thans</a>, maer <a href = vnd.unilang:ick.html>ick</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:al.html>al</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:lang.html>lang</a> sien <a href = vnd.unilang:vallen.html>vallen</a>:<br /><a href = vnd.unilang:van.html>Van</a> zedert <a href = vnd.unilang:soo.html>soo</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:verwoed.html>verwoed</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:rondom.html>rondom</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> staende <a href = vnd.unilang:wallen.html>wallen</a>,<br /><a href = vnd.unilang:met.html>Met</a> sijn' <b><a href = vnd.unilang:strijdwagen.html>strijdwagen</a></b> styf, <a href = vnd.unilang:en.html>en</a> wacker aengesweept,<br /><a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>De</a> wreede Peleus soon <a href = vnd.unilang:mijn.html>mijn</a>' <a href = vnd.unilang:leden.html>leden</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:heeft.html>heeft</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:gesleept.html>gesleept</a>:</span><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">You have old <a href = vnd.unilang:troy.html>Troy</a> for now, but I [have] long seen it fall<br />From since, so enraged, round the [still] standing walls,<br />With his sturdy <b>chariot</b> and driven fiercely,<br />The cruel son of Peleus <a href = vnd.unilang:has.html>has</a> dragged my [better <a href = vnd.unilang:half.html>half</a>'s] body:</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li></ul></li></ol>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Zelfstandig_naamwoord"><i><a href = vnd.unilang:zelfstandig.html>Zelfstandig</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:naamwoord.html>naamwoord</a></i></span></h4>

<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">stric</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">stricke</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">strec</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">stric</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*strikkiz</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">line; rope</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*streyg-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">stiff; rigid; tight; rope; cord</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*(s)ter-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">stiff</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.

***strikken.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:strikken.html>strikken</a> (11713)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">stricken</i>. Equivalent to <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:strik.html>strik</a></i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">-en</i>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:strikken.html>strikken</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li>to tie (up a shoelace for example)</li>
<li>to get (someone to do something for you); to ask to stay
<dl><dd><i><a href = vnd.unilang:ik.html>Ik</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:probeerde.html>probeerde</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:haar.html>haar</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:al.html>al</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:langer.html>langer</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:te.html>te</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:strikken.html>strikken</a></b>.</i>: I tried to get her to stay a bit longer.</dd></dl></li></ol>

<p>See the etymology of the main entry.

<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">struuf</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*strūf</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*strūbaz</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">stiff, rough, bristly, <a href = vnd.unilang:shaggy.html>shaggy</a></span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*strewbʰ-</i>, <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*strewb-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">stiff</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. Cognate with <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Low_German" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Low German">Middle Low German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="gml">struuf</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/West_Frisian_language" class="extiw" title="w:West Frisian language">West Frisian</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fy"><a href = vnd.unilang:stroef.html>stroef</a></i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">straub</i> and <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">struppig</i>.

<ol><li>rough, not smooth</li>

<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_High_German" class="extiw" title="w:Middle High German">Middle High German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="gmh">strāfen</i>. </p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="lb"><a href = vnd.unilang:strofen.html>strofen</a></strong> (<i>third-person singular present</i> <b class="Latn" lang="lb">strooft</b>, <i>past participle</i> <b class="Latn" lang="lb">gestrooft</b>, <i>auxiliary verb</i> <b class="Latn" lang="lb">hunn</b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to punish
<ul><li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>2013</b>,  <a href = vnd.unilang:christiane.html>Christiane</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> Bricasart,  <cite>Wann d'Rous sech verstoppt fir <a href = vnd.unilang:ze.html>ze</a> kräischen</cite>, <small>→ISBN</small>, page 14:</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Latn e-quotation" lang="lb"><i>Fir mäi Behuelen gouf <a href = vnd.unilang:ech.html>ech</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:vu.html>vu</a> menger Mamm <b>gestrooft</b>, si huet mech ugestallt hir <a href = vnd.unilang:bei.html>bei</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:der.html>der</a> grousser Wäsch an <a href = vnd.unilang:der.html>der</a> Wäschkichen <a href = vnd.unilang:ze.html>ze</a> hëllefen.</i></span><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">For my behaviour I <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a> <b>punished</b> by my mother; she ordered <a href = vnd.unilang:me.html>me</a> to help her in the laundry room during the big wash.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></div></li></ul></li></ol>

***stroganoff.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:stroganoff.html>stroganoff</a> (33784)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Named after the Stroganov family, a distinguished Russian family involved in the settlement of Siberia, <span class="etylcleanup"><span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Russian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Russian language">Russian</a></span></span> <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">стро́ганов</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">Stróganov</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:stroganoff.html>stroganoff</a></strong> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en">stroganoffs</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>A dish of sautéed pieces of beef (or a substitute) served in a sauce with sour cream.
<ul><li><b>2002</b>, Hope Ricciotti, <a href = vnd.unilang:vincent.html>Vincent</a> Connelly, <i>The Pregnancy Cookbook</i>.
<dl><dd>With its creamy texture and unique taste, our version <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> certain to win <a href = vnd.unilang:over.html>over</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:even.html>even</a> the most diehard <b><a href = vnd.unilang:stroganoff.html>stroganoff</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:fans.html>fans</a>.</dd></dl></li>
<li><b>1999</b>, John Yeoman, <i>Self Reliance: A Recipe for the New Millennium</i>.
<dl><dd>For an unusual kidney <b><a href = vnd.unilang:stroganoff.html>stroganoff</a></b>, saute them in a <a href = vnd.unilang:casserole.html>casserole</a> with chopped onions, celery and carrot, then stew in wine, <a href = vnd.unilang:beer.html>beer</a>, cider or stock till tender, and stir in a little cream before serving.</dd></dl></li></ul></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><i><a href = vnd.unilang:stroganoff.html>Stroganoff</a></i> <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> sometimes, but not always, capitalised. Although it may originally have functioned as an adjective following the noun <i>beef</i>, it <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> now often regarded as a noun in itself, just as preparations of chicken <a href = vnd.unilang:kiev.html>Kiev</a> are now frequently referred to as kievs.
</p>
</body>

</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:stroming.html>stroming</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:stromingen.html>stromingen</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:stroming.html>strominkje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li>a stream</li>
<li>a flow, current
<dl><dd><i><a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>De</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:stroming.html>stroming</a></b> in <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:mantel.html>mantel</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:veroorzaakt.html>veroorzaakt</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:bewegingen.html>bewegingen</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:van.html>van</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:platen.html>platen</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:en.html>en</a> vulkanisme <a href = vnd.unilang:aan.html>aan</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:het.html>het</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:aardoppervlak.html>aardoppervlak</a>.</i><sup id="cite_ref-1" class="reference"><a href="cite_note-1"> | 1 | </a></sup>  |  The flow in the <a href = vnd.unilang:mantle.html>mantle</a> causes the movements of the plates and volcanism on the Earth's surface.</dd></dl></li>
<li>a movement (e.g. cultural, social, or artistic)</li>
<li>a school of thought</li></ol>

***stront.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:stront.html>stront</a> (2189)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:stront.html>stront</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss"><a href = vnd.unilang:shit.html>shit</a>, dreck, manure</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*strunt</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">excrement, turd, <a href = vnd.unilang:shit.html>shit</a></span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. <span class="maintenance-line"><i>This etymology <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> incomplete. You can help Wiktionary by elaborating on the origins of this term.</i></span>
</p><p>Compare <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/French_language" class="extiw" title="w:French language">French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fr">étron</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">turd, crap</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Italian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Italian language">Italian</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="it">stronzo</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">turd, crap</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. Cognate with <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/English_language" class="extiw" title="w:English language">English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">strunt</i>.
</p>

<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">strôom</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*strōm</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*straumaz</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*srew-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to flow</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.

***structuur.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:structuur.html>structuur</a> (7316)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_French" class="extiw" title="w:Middle French">Middle French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="frm">structure</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">structura</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">a fitting together, adjustment, building, erection, a building, edifice, structure</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">structus</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">pile up, arrange, assemble, build</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, past participle of <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">struere</i>. Compare <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">construct</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">instruct</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">destroy</i>, etc.

<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:struikrover.html>struikrover</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:struikrovers.html>struikrovers</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:struikrover.html>struikrovertje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="Latn" lang="en">highwayman</span>, literally one who ambushes their victims from behind the <a href = vnd.unilang:bushes.html>bushes</a></li></ol>

***struisvogel.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:struisvogel.html>struisvogel</a> (42998)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Compound of <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:struis.html>struis</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">ostrich</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:vogel.html>vogel</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">bird</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. Attested since the 17th century, displacing earlier <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">vogelstruis</i>. The element <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:struis.html>struis</a></i> derives from Latin <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">strūthiō</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:struisvogel.html>struisvogel</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:struisvogels.html>struisvogels</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:struisvogel.html>struisvogeltje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li>An ostrich, flightless bird of the genus <i>Struthio</i>.
<dl><dd><span class="nyms synonym"><span class="defdate">Synonym:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="nl">vogelstruis</span></span></dd></dl></li></ol>

<li><span class="Latn" lang="nl">struisvogelei</span></li>

***struisvogelpolitiek.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:struisvogelpolitiek.html>struisvogelpolitiek</a> (79225)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From of <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:struisvogel.html>struisvogel</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">ostrich</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:politiek.html>politiek</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">politics</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, possibly a calque of calque of  <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">Vogel-Strauß-Politik</i>. Named after the common misconception that ostriches bury their heads in the sand when confronted with danger. First attested in 1848.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:struisvogelpolitiek.html>struisvogelpolitiek</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr></span> (<i>uncountable</i>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">derogatory</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> An evasive style of politics that fails to address problems by either ignoring them or by creating a false sense of security through (known) ineffective measures; <span class="Latn" lang="en">ostrich politics</span>.
<ul><li><b>1848</b> August 24, Æneas Mackay, quoted in "<a href = vnd.unilang:voortzetting.html>Voortzetting</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:der.html>der</a> beraadslagingen <a href = vnd.unilang:over.html>over</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:herziening.html>Herziening</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:der.html>der</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:grondwet.html>Grondwet</a>", <i>Bijvoegsel <a href = vnd.unilang:tot.html>tot</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:nieuwe.html>Nieuwe</a> Rotterdamsche <a href = vnd.unilang:courant.html>Courant</a></i>, issue 202, page 2.
<dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Latn e-quotation" lang="nl">Z.Exc. <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> minister <a href = vnd.unilang:van.html>van</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:justitie.html>justitie</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:heeft.html>heeft</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:dien.html>dien</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:vijand.html>vijand</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:met.html>met</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:moed.html>moed</a> in '<a href = vnd.unilang:t.html>t</a> aangezigt <a href = vnd.unilang:gezien.html>gezien</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:en.html>en</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:niet.html>niet</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:die.html>die</a> <i><b><a href = vnd.unilang:struisvogelpolitiek.html>struisvogelpolitiek</a></b></i> <a href = vnd.unilang:gevolgd.html>gevolgd</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:maar.html>maar</a> den <a href = vnd.unilang:vijand.html>vijand</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:te.html>te</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:gemoeten.html>gemoet</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:gegaan.html>gegaan</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:met.html>met</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:grondwet.html>grondwet</a> in <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> hand.</span><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">His Excellency the Minister of Justice <a href = vnd.unilang:has.html>has</a> looked that enemy in the face with courage, and hasn'<a href = vnd.unilang:t.html>t</a> followed those <b>ostrich politics</b>, but approached the enemy with the constitution in his hand.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li></ul></li></ol>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Zelfstandig_naamwoord"><i><a href = vnd.unilang:zelfstandig.html>Zelfstandig</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:naamwoord.html>naamwoord</a></i></span></h4>
<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:struisvogelpolitiek.html>struisvogelpolitiek</a></b> <span style="background-color: f8f9fa;border-radius: 2px;border: 1px solid c8ccd1;padding: 0 0.2em 0 0.1em;font-style: italic">v</span>
</p>
<ol><li><span style="background-color:FFFFE0;font-style: italic;">(<a href = vnd.unilang:politiek.html>politiek</a>)</span> handelwijze <a href = vnd.unilang:waarbij.html>waarbij</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:men.html>men</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:het.html>het</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:gevaar.html>gevaar</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:niet.html>niet</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:onder.html>onder</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:ogen.html>ogen</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:wil.html>wil</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:zien.html>zien</a>. <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>De</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:uitdrukking.html>uitdrukking</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:berust.html>berust</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:op.html>op</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:het.html>het</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:onterechte.html>onterechte</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:geloof.html>geloof</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:dat.html>dat</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:struisvogels.html>struisvogels</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:hun.html>hun</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:kop.html>kop</a> in <a href = vnd.unilang:het.html>het</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:zand.html>zand</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:steken.html>steken</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:als.html>als</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:ze.html>ze</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:zich.html>zich</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:bedreigd.html>bedreigd</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:voelen.html>voelen</a></li></ol>

<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:studie.html>studie</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">studium</i>.
